<p><i>Our People &amp; Places Solutions business – reinforces our drive to improve the lives of people everywhere and epitomizes the \"why\" of what we do – the tremendous positive impact and value our solutions bring to our communities and society as a whole. From facilities delivering life-saving therapies and ensuring clean water to enabling the connection of people through all modes of transportation and providing access to technology – we're integrating a multitude of these solution elements to build the smart environments of tomorrow.<\u002Fi><br> <br> <i>Start your Jacobs career with a company that inspires and empowers you to deliver your best work so you can evolve, grow and succeed – today and into tomorrow.<\u002Fi><\u002Fp>\n <br> \n <br> \n <b>Your Impact:<\u002Fb>\n <p><br> At Jacobs, we’re helping our clients innovate and grow by designing, engineering, and executing the construction of their various facilities that are changing our world. Our talented experts create exceptional spaces across the world through our creative blending of human need, environmental stewardship, value creation, science and art. We believe that built environments should reflect the context, history, cultures, communities, and the natural environment while incorporating advances in technology.<\u002Fp> \n <p>Our Water business would like to welcome you to be part of an Advanced Meter Infrastructure (AMI) project as a Site Inspector. You will be part of an exciting water meter digitalization project across Singapore.<\u002Fp> \n <p>This Site Inspector role will inspect the installation, testing, commissioning and monitoring of Advanced Metering Infrastructure (AMI) Smart meters as part of the AMI Demonstration Project. The Inspector should have an interest in water metering systems, plumbing system with local regulatory requirement, and wireless communication, M&amp;E installation for smart meters, as well as IT skills. The Inspector role includes oversight and supervision of meters across Singapore. Weekly reports on the data and statistics will be required with OMNI Software tools and reporting to Site Engineers, Functional and Project Managers.<\u002Fp> \n <p>Reporting to the Site Engineers (SE), Project Manager and the Implementation Manager. Responsible for standing supervision of the installation works and verification of the AMI meter performance against an agreed set of criteria with the client. Essential Duties:<\u002Fp> \n <ul>\n  <li>Initial oversight of configuration and successful installation and commissioning of AMI meters distributed across Singapore.<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Ongoing oversight and documentation of results including communication signal strength, signal quality, alarms, noise and alerts.<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Verify meter data through Meter Data Management System (MDMS) and correctness of data to the Electronic Billing System (EBS).<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Oversee Contractor’s installation against contract specifications and requirements.<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Prepare reports, alert the client and Jacobs of any pending issues, and make recommendations on the project’s success.<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Inspectors to support the SEs in the direct monitoring of the AMI contractor and they shall be present in Singapore for the duration of the assignment.<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Each Inspector shall carry out preferably same-day quality supervision and assurance site checks on 100% of the meter installation\u002Freplacement works performed by the AMI contractor and report deficiencies to the SEs.<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Each Inspector shall validate newly installed hardware information (such as meter serial numbers and meter readings) preferably electronically as well as perform an assessment of the as-left site condition, any irregularities (such as leaking valves) as well as rectification works by AMI contractor.<\u002Fli> \n <\u002Ful>\n <b>Here’s What You’ll Need:<\u002Fb>\n <p><br> To be a successful candidate you shall possess:<\u002Fp> \n <ul>\n  <li>Minimum ITE Diploma in Mechanical \u002F Electrical \u002F Instrumentation Control and Automation or equivalent<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Minimum 2 years of relevant working experience in overseeing\u002Fsupervising site\u002Ffield works or construction management<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Familiar with local regulatory requirements<\u002Fli> \n  <li>A Singaporean working right<\u002Fli> \n <\u002Ful>\n <p><b>Jacobs.
